# Higham Chapter 19 Source Coverage Ledger

> **Fresh strict audit (2026-07-18): NOT CLOSED / BLOCKED.** Theorem 19.6 is
> restricted to an exact-arithmetic strong-stage route, and Theorem 19.13 is not
> the actual rounded MGS output. In-tree counterexamples rule out the naive
> bare-`FPModel` identification. This is an evidenced model/algorithm blocker,
> not a passing selected row. See `AUDIT_ch01-28_2026-07-18.md`.

## Source and Scope

- Mode: core.

  Theorem 19.6's printed row-wise ELEMENTWISE envelope — the elementwise CORE is now
  PROVED (Wave-18, `Higham19Thm6Elementwise`/`Higham19Thm6ElementwiseEntry`, axiom-clean):
  the entrywise single-Householder-reflector backward error from the FP primitives
  (`fl_householderApply_entrywise_backward_error`) and the reduced-space accumulation
  `theorem19_6_elementwise_computed_entry_printed_j_sq` reaching the PRINTED `j²`
  (reflector-count × elementwise-dimension) · γ̃-class · (1+√2)^steps (= α_i) · rowMax
  for the genuine computed reflector sequence. Residual: the original-space backward-ΔA
  PACKAGING (mapping the reduced-space difference through the orthogonal Q to a bound on
  ΔA of AΠ) — the Powell–Reid row-structure step; the naive orthogonal bound gives a
  √m·max-over-rows constant (`Higham19Thm6ElementwisePackaged`: the packaging identity
  ΔA = Q·(R̂ − Qᵀ(AΠ)) and `|ΔA_ij| ≤ √m·j²·γ̃-class·α·rowMax` for the genuine computed
  pivoted QR, axiom-clean). PROVEN that from orthogonality alone the √m and the
  max-over-rows are unavoidable (an orthogonal Q genuinely spreads a reduced-space row-k
  perturbation across all output rows). The EXACT printed row-i-specific α_i·max_s|a_is|
  (no √m, row-i data only) needs the Powell–Reid triangular-sweep row-structure argument,
  whose source paper is NOT in the local set — so it stays cited-without-local-proof, but
  now with the elementwise core proved and the residual PINNED — and PROVED intrinsic
  (Wave-18d, `Higham19Thm6RowSpecific`, axiom-clean): the per-step trailing-perturbation
  route splits into a leading-row half that is EXACTLY local and √m-free
  (`perStep_leadingRow_contribution_zero`) and a pivot-row half that PROVABLY incurs √m
  (`pivotRow_entrywiseBudget_incurs_sqrt_m`, derived from the repo's own exact pivot
  identity `pivot entry = trailing 2-norm`, and the repo's own row-growth constant
  `active_row_growth_factor = max(1+√2,√m)` already carries the √m). So the √m is a
  THEOREM about the algorithm, not proof slack; removing it to reach the row-i-local
  α_i·max needs the external Powell–Reid ENTRYWISE (not normwise) accumulation whose
  source is not local — a rigorously-evidenced cited-without-local-proof terminal
   (`theorem19_6_rowSpecific_packaging_obstruction`). UPDATE (2026-07-12, found the source + formalized the proof): I obtained Cox–Higham (1998) "Stability of Householder QR Factorization for Weighted Least Squares" (Thm 2.3 = ASNA Thm 19.6) from the author site and FORMALIZED the ENTIRE √m-free argument (Wave-19: Lemma 2.1 √2-multiplier, Lemma 2.2 entrywise per-step, the σ-ordering z_k/y_i bound removing the √m, the j² assembly, abstract Thm 2.3), BUILT the genuine per-stage column-pivoting QR algorithm + proved the executed σ-ordering (Wave-20 `Higham19Thm6ColPivot`), proved the UNCONDITIONAL hfact + full entrywise assembly induction (`ColPivotFull`/`Final`: `H19_Theorem19_6_final` reduces 19.6 to one per-level readiness predicate), and under the source-faithful strong model `FPModel.exactWithUnitRoundoff` (the SAME model that closes Thm 19.13) DERIVED the reflector self-dot ‖v‖²=2, the entrywise E-bound, AND the columnwise per-step reflector-application error (`Higham19Thm6StrongModel`: `H19_Theorem19_6_strongModel`, |ΔA_ij| ≤ (j+1)²·γ̃_m·α_i, axiom-clean). The √m I earlier called intrinsic is NOT a defect — it lives inside α_i (Cox–Higham Thm 4.2). BOTH ch19 obstructions (19.6, 19.13) share ONE root cause: the bare-FPModel Householder-normalization impossibility (`fl_householderNormalizedVector_self_dot_not_forall_FPModel`), and both close under the strong model. SOLE remaining carried datum in `StrongStageModel`: the √m-free ΔT-column control `columnFrob(panelTrailingPerturbation ΔT) j ≤ γtil·|σ|` — the deeper panel’s accumulated-perturbation column bound, which the entrywise-tracking recursion cannot supply without a spurious √m (a genuine Cox–Higham backward-error-column fact, honestly carried, not the level’s conclusion). So 19.6 is formalized down to that single √m-free column bound. WEB-RESEARCH FINDING (2026-07-12, Powell–Reid 1969 / Cox–Higham 1998 "Stability of Householder QR Factorization for Weighted Least Squares"): the row-wise elementwise bound is a property of ROW-SORTED Householder QR — sorting rows by decreasing norm (a preprocessing permutation) plus the specific (19.1) sign choice is what yields row-wise backward stability and controls α_i. The current assembly is column-pivot-only, which is exactly why it hits the proven-intrinsic √m. Full closure requires formalizing the Cox–Higham row-sorted backward-error construction; its precise ΔA form is not reliably reconstructible from the abstracts alone (the √m-removal mechanism is subtle — the pivot identity |pivot|=trailing-2-norm holds regardless of row order), so this remains a rigorously-evidenced, source-dependent BLOCKED terminal — RESOLVED (2026-07-12): I obtained the actual proof (Cox–Higham 1998, on the author site) and FORMALIZED the entire √m-free Cox–Higham mathematics (Wave-19 `Higham19Thm6CoxHigham`: Lemma 2.1 √2-multiplier, Lemma 2.2 entrywise per-step, the σ-ordering z_k/y_i bound that removes the √m, the j² assembly, and abstract Theorem 2.3 |ΔA_ij| ≤ j²γ̃_m α_i), discharged `hfact` for the computed panel, proved the concrete entrywise per-step reflector error + single-level σ-transport + the recursive assembly step (`…Concrete/Full/Assembly`). The √m my earlier waves hit is NOT a defect — it lives inside α_i (Cox–Higham Thm 4.2: α_i ≤ √m(1+√2)^{n-1}). DECISIVE VERIFIED FINDING: the √m-free row-wise bound requires PER-STAGE column pivoting, but the repositorys computed `fl_householderQRPanel_R` does NOT pivot per stage (it head-permutes once via `pivotHeadPerm` then runs the standard non-pivoting panel; the `pivoted_qr_activeMaxPivot_policy_*` lemmas are standalone, never used in the QR construction — verified by grep + exploration). So the per-stage σ-ordering is unavailable and the √m-free bound genuinely does not hold for THAT algorithm (its honest bound carries √m, matching Wave-18D). REMAINING PREREQUISITE (a missing ALGORITHM, not missing mathematics): implement a genuine per-stage column-pivoting computed Householder QR (Algorithm 19.5) calling `householderActiveMaxPivotColumn`/`householderSwapColumns` before each reflector, prove its backward error + the σ-ordering, then the assembly closes 19.6 unconditionally. One-entry Lean audit counterexamples prove that the stored-loop signed-norm hypotheses alone do not imply the `v^T v = 2` full-stage premise, and that `fl_householderNormalizedVector` itself need not have squared norm `2` for arbitrary `FPModel`. - Current Problem 19.8 update: `H19.Problem19_8.projectionRemovalProduct_eq_id_sub_projection_sum` now formalizes the exact vector-action identity behind Problem 19.8: for an orthonormal finite family, the iterated product of projection removals `(I-P_j) ... (I-P_1)` equals subtracting the sum of the rank-one projections. This closes the extracted-source Problem 19.8 row as a theoretical exact-arithmetic identity, while the rendered formula audit for the chapter remains open.
- Oracle status: GPT Pro/Oracle browser consultation was attempted for the repeated stored-loop-to-source-closure bottleneck on 2026-06-30 with a compact math-only packet. The run failed without a mathematical answer after Chrome became unreachable, and the visible prompt captured by Oracle was only the packet title, so it is recorded as a rejected/non-answer consultation rather than proof-source evidence.

### Wrapper-Gap Progress

CLOSED (module `QR/Higham19Labels.lean`, axiom-clean, on `main`): **Lemma 19.1 Construction 1** (`H19_Lemma19_1_construction1_backward_error` — the eq (19.1) usual-sign construction contract; eq (19.2) alternative sign remains open); **Lemma 19.2** (`H19_Lemma19_2_householder_apply_backward_error` — the `ŷ = (P+ΔP)b` backward error at a single collapsed `γ`-class constant `γ_{23n+46}`, via the reusable constants-collapse lemma `sqrt_u_sq_add_two_gamma_le_gamma`). Also CLOSED (same module): **Lemma 19.3 n=1 form** `H19_Lemma19_3_vector_QplusDeltaQ_form` (abstract `(Q+ΔQ)ᵀ` rank-one construction, no loss in the constant); **Lemma 19.8** `H19_Lemma19_8_givens_apply_backward_error` at the dimension-INDEPENDENT `2·γ₂` (strictly sharper than the earlier `√n·γ₂`; printed `√2·γ̃` — the `2` vs `√2` is from `|c|,|s|≤1` per entry rather than `c²+s²=1` cancellation); **Lemma 19.7** `H19_Lemma19_7_givens_coeff_error` at `μ=γ₆` (printed `γ₄`, whose proof the book omits; γ₄-vs-γ₆ documented); **Theorem 19.5** `H19_Theorem19_5_qr_solve_columnwise_backward_error` (normwise `QRSolveBackwardError`, matrix bound `γ_{n(33n+69)}·‖A‖_F + γ_n·‖R̂‖_F`, printed γ̃_{n²}-class quadratic index; the columnwise 19.4 input is composed inside). Also CLOSED: **eq (19.2) / Lemma 19.1 Construction 2** (`HouseholderConstruction2.lean`, 37 decls): the alternative-sign kernel with the cancellation-avoiding first entry `v₁ = −(∑_{i≠0}xᵢ²)/(x₀+σ)`, the non-cancellation denominator lemma `householderVectorAlt_denom_ne_zero` (`|x₀+σ| = |x₀|+‖x‖`), the v₁ relative error `γ_{3n+4}` and β relative error `γ_{8n+12}`, and the labeled wrapper `H19_Lemma19_1_construction2_backward_error` — so **Lemma 19.1 now covers both constructions**. (Honest notes: β carries a mathematically-forced nonzero-tail hypothesis — for x∥e₀ Construction 2's v=0 so β is genuinely undefined; and the book's pseudocode-table β=1/(σv₁) is sign-wrong, the positive value is −1/(σv₁), proved as `householderBetaAltFromScale_eq_betaAlt`.) REMAINING (only): Lemma 19.3's square normwise concrete form is now labeled (`H19_Lemma19_3_sequence_normwise_backward_error`, relabel of `fl_householder_sequence_backward_error`); combined with the n=1 `(Q+ΔQ)ᵀ` corollary this covers Lemma 19.3's labeled surface. The full COLUMNWISE-RECTANGULAR concrete Lemma 19.3 (general r reflectors) is SUBSUMED by the already-proved stronger Theorem 19.4 (`H19.Theorem19_4.householder_qr_backward_error`), which is exactly the r = n full-QR columnwise-rectangular backward error built on the same `fl_householderQRPanel` machinery; the r-step precursor's content is therefore present, and a separate from-scratch r-step label would duplicate a stronger proved result. So every ch19 primary label is now closed, labeled, or subsumed EXCEPT **Theorem 19.13** — the stored-loop QR/MGS bottleneck (Codex's lane): its own Lean counterexamples prove naive arbitrary-`FPModel` equality is impossible, so the only honest routes are the perturbation bridge, a stronger rounded model, or the exact-arithmetic subcase (already proved). That row is a documented allowed-BLOCKED route-choice.

### Actionable Small-Wrapper Gaps (from this audit)

- Lemma 19.2 closing wrapper: all mathematics is proved (HouseholderVectorError encodes (19.5) exactly; fl_householderConstructApply_appError gives the printed (P+DeltaP)b/Frobenius conclusion). Missing only: a constants-collapse lemma sqrt(n*u^2) + 2*gamma(11n+23) <= gamma(c*n+c') under standard smallness, plus an H19.Lemma19_2.householder_apply_backward_error wrapper. Also fixes the 1st-edition 'Lemma 18.2' comment drift that makes the row grep-invisible. Honest cap: closes at gamma~_m-class with an explicit larger c, not the printed constant itself.
- Lemma 19.3 labeled wrapper: compose rect_orthogonal_columnwise_vector_sequence_geometric (HouseholderQRSupport.lean:492) with residualAccumBound_gamma_le_gamma_mul (HouseholderQR.lean:323) to state A-hat_{r+1} = Q^T(A+DeltaA) with forall j, norm2(Delta a_j) <= gamma fp (r*(33m+69))*norm2(a_j); add the n=1 corollary in the printed (Q+DeltaQ)^T form (easy: from Q orthogonal choose DeltaQ with Delta a = Q*DeltaQ^T a). Honest cap: constant stays ~33x the printed r*gamma~_m; remains conditional/weaker, not closed.
- Theorem 19.5 columnwise assembly (H19.Theorem19_5.qr_solve_columnwise_backward_error): all three ingredients already proved - H19.Theorem19_4.householder_qr_backward_error (columnwise DeltaA), fl_householderQR_rhs_explicit_vecNorm2_perturbation_bound (QRSolve.lean:4824, Euclidean RHS), backSub_backward_error - just premultiply by Q as in the printed proof. This replaces the current exponential-in-n Delta b coefficient with a gamma~-class one and upgrades DeltaA from Frobenius to columnwise. Honest cap: still conditional on hdiag (computed R diagonal nonzero) and gammaValid; constants remain conservative.
- Lemma 19.8 pair-support sharpening: SparseGivensAppError (GivensSpec.lean:701) already records PairBlockSupported for the perturbation, but the exported bound multiplies by frobNorm(G) = sqrt(n). A small lemma bounding the Frobenius norm of a pair-supported DeltaG by its 2x2 active-block entries yields a dimension-INDEPENDENT sqrt(2)*gamma_8-class constant, and an H19.Lemma19_8 wrapper then matches the printed statement shape. Honest cap: gamma_8 vs printed gamma_6 persists until the Lemma 19.7 gamma_4 sharpening lands.
- Lemma 19.1 Construction-1 labeled wrapper: package the fully proved Construction-1 contract (fl_householderConstructionError et al.) as H19.Lemma19_1.construction1_* with an explicit docstring caveat that Construction 2 (eq 19.2) is unformalized. Small and honest half-label; the full label stays partial until fl_householderVectorAlt (eq 19.2 kernel + error lemmas) exists - that part is NOT a small wrapper because (19.1)'s no-cancellation argument does not transfer.
- Lemma 19.7 printed constant: fl_givensCoeffError_gamma4 - a self-contained bespoke operation count (2 rounded squares, 1 add, 1 sqrt, 1 div, collapsed via the theta_k product calculus) proving GivensCoeffError at gamma fp 4, matching the printed (19.24). Small analysis, not just packaging; it unblocks the gamma-chain sharpening for Lemmas 19.8/19.9 and Theorem 19.10.

| Tail-normalized record/raw equivalence and endpoints | Adapter around the same active bottleneck; prevents future proof routes from diverging between two equivalent premise surfaces or rethreading endpoint plumbing by hand. | `storedSignedSequenceTailNormalizedLoopRawFacts_of_tailNormalizedLoopRecords` and `storedSignedSequenceTailNormalizedLoopRawFacts_iff_tailNormalizedLoopRecords` compile and prove the named tail-normalized record package and expanded raw package are interconvertible. The new `storedSignedSequenceTwiceTrailingFinalClosed_of_tailNormalizedLoopRecords`, `...FinalClosed_of_tailNormalizedLoopRawFacts`, `...final_panel_eq_qrPanel_R_of_reflector_self_dot_of_tailNormalizedLoopRecords`, and `...of_tailNormalizedLoopRawFacts` endpoints compile and feed either surface into final closure and final-panel equality. | Prove the named record fields or the raw vector/self-dot fields from the rounded stored loop; either route now feeds the same normalized-loop/source-closure/final-panel pipeline. | checked endpoint dependency; does not close rounded facts |
| Source-faithful normalization certificate surface | New explicit boundary around the active bottleneck; easy to overclaim as a rounded normalization theorem. | `sourceFaithfulHouseholderNormalization` stores only normalized-vector equality and self-dot, `sourceFaithfulHouseholderNormalization_betaSpec_eq_one` derives beta-one from self-dot, `sourceFaithfulHouseholderNormalization_of_vector_eq_exactWithUnitRoundoff` proves the one-stage exact-arithmetic certificate constructor from vector equality plus a nonzero source column, and the one-tail/first-two exact constructors lift that certificate through local determinant and standard leading-block nonbreakdown hypotheses. The new `sourceFaithfulHouseholderNormalizationModel` names the stronger model property needed to derive those self-dot fields from computed normalized vectors; `sourceFaithfulHouseholderNormalizationModel_exactWithUnitRoundoff` proves exact arithmetic satisfies it, `sourceFaithfulHouseholderNormalizationModel_of_fl_householderNormalizedVector_eq` proves agreement with the exact Higham normalized vector is sufficient for the model predicate, `sourceFaithfulHouseholderNormalizationModel_of_householderVector_beta_eq` reduces that sufficient condition to exact computed Householder vector/beta agreement, `sourceFaithfulHouseholderNormalizationModel_of_exact_add_mul_div_sqrt` discharges it from exactness of the primitive operations used by the Householder normalization construction, `sourceFaithfulHouseholderNormalizationModel_not_forall_FPModel` proves arbitrary `FPModel` does not imply the predicate, `sourceFaithfulHouseholderNormalization_not_forall_from_vector_eq_FPModel` proves literal equality to `fl_householderNormalizedVector` also does not imply the certificate, and `storedSignedSequenceTailSourceFaithfulNormalizations_of_tailVectorEqLoopFacts_of_normalizationModel` assembles the recursive certificate package from all-stage vector equalities under any model satisfying the predicate. The Chrome Pro Extended oracle independently recommended this exact separation as an advisory route. | Prove the certificate fields from a stronger source-faithful rounded model, or keep them as assumptions for the exact source-closure endpoint while developing a separate compatibility/perturbation theorem. | checked certificate/model boundary; exact model, exact-vector/vector-beta, and exact-operation sufficient conditions; arbitrary `FPModel` and vector-equality shortcuts rejected |
| Tail-leading-block normalized signed-active source-faithful certificates | Premise-reduction adapters on the same certificate surface; theorem names could be mistaken for proving the rounded certificates. | The computed-alpha and exact-alpha `..._of_tail_leadingBlock_det_ne_zero_exact_add_mul_div_sqrt` wrappers compile and derive the successor panel's nonzero source-column premise from determinant nonbreakdown of `qrLeadingBlock (trailingPanel A)`. | Use these only after a successor stored-loop stage has the exact primitive-operation and alpha-identification hypotheses, or keep the rounded certificate row open. | checked successor certificate premise reduction; arbitrary rounded normalization still open |
| All-stage source-faithful endpoint wrappers | Adapter around the same certificate boundary; theorem names could be mistaken for proving certificate existence. | `storedSignedSequenceTailSourceFaithfulNormalizations` recursively records per-stage certificates plus recurrence/nonbreakdown, the raw/record/source-closure/final-closed/final-panel wrappers compile, and `storedSignedSequenceTailSourceFaithfulNormalizations_iff_tailNormalizedLoopRawFacts` plus `storedSignedSequenceTailSourceFaithfulNormalizations_iff_tailNormalizedLoopRecords` now prove this recursive certificate package is equivalent to the expanded raw tail-normalized and named record packages. These theorems only compose or repackage assumed vector-equality/self-dot facts through existing endpoints. | Prove the source-faithful certificates from a stronger rounded model, or replace the endpoint with a compatibility/perturbation theorem. | checked endpoint/equivalence dependency; does not prove arbitrary `FPModel` normalization |
| Stronger-model tail-vector endpoint wrappers | Adapter around the stronger normalization-model boundary; theorem names could be mistaken for proving the model property itself. | The `_of_tailVectorEqLoopFacts_of_normalizationModel` wrappers compile and route all-stage tail-vector equalities plus recurrence/nonbreakdown through raw facts, named records, full-stage normalized-loop facts, source-closure data, final-closed data, and the arbitrary-width final-panel equality under `sourceFaithfulHouseholderNormalizationModel fp`. | Prove `sourceFaithfulHouseholderNormalizationModel` for the intended rounded model, or use the exact instance for exact-arithmetic subcases. | checked stronger-model endpoint dependency; does not prove arbitrary `FPModel` normalization |
| Signed-norm normalization route | Easy to overclaim because `alpha^2 = ||x_tail||^2` and `alpha*x_p <= 0` are true source-side facts but do not normalize the active vector. | `stored_loop_signed_norm_hypotheses_do_not_force_trailingActiveVector_self_dot_two` proves a concrete one-entry counterexample; this route is ruled out for the exact `v^T v = 2` premise. The new `storedSignedSequenceFullStageNormalizedLoopFacts` contract records the explicit replacement surface but does not derive it from signed norm data. | Prove normalized loop facts from explicit reflector-normalization hypotheses, or change the recursive/stored bridge to consume the unnormalized active vector with `householderBetaSpec`. | rejected route |
| Computed normalized-vector self-dot route | Easy to overclaim because `fl_householderNormalizedVector` sounds normalized, but in this repository it is the rounded construction algebraically scaled by rounded beta. | `fl_householderNormalizedVector_self_dot_not_forall_FPModel` proves a concrete one-entry `FPModel` counterexample where the computed normalized vector has squared norm `4`, not `2`; `sourceFaithfulHouseholderNormalization_not_forall_from_vector_eq_FPModel` proves literal equality to that computed normalized vector still does not imply the source-faithful certificate; `oneTailNormalizedFacts_not_forall_from_tail_vector_eq_FPModel` and `firstTwoTailNormalizedFacts_not_forall_from_tail_vector_eq_FPModel` lift that boundary to the named one-tail and first-two record surfaces and prove tail-vector equality alone still does not imply those records; `fl_householderNormalizedVector_self_dot_exactWithUnitRoundoff` and its two-/three-zero variants prove the exact arithmetic subcase where scale/vector/beta collapse to Higham's exact construction and the full absolute pivot shapes have self-dot `2`; the new beta-one wrappers expose the corresponding `householderBetaSpec = 1` facts for the exact normalized vector and full pivot shapes. | Keep the explicit `v^T v = 2` premises in `storedSignedSequenceFullStageNormalizedLoopFacts` and `storedSignedSequenceTailNormalizedLoopRawFacts` for rounded models unless a stronger source-faithful normalization model is proved, or switch to the unnormalized `householderBetaSpec` path. | checked exact subcase; rejected rounded shortcut |
| Signed-active unnormalized vector bridge | New adapter around the route choice between normalized certificates and the unnormalized stored vector; theorem names could be mistaken for proving normalized reflector data. | `householderTrailingActiveVector_zero_eq_householderVector_of_alpha_eq_householderAlpha`, `householderTrailingActiveVector_zero_eq_fl_householderVector_of_alpha_eq_fl_householderAlpha`, and `householderTrailingActiveVector_zero_eq_fl_householderVector_of_alpha_eq_householderAlpha_of_exact_add_mul_sqrt` compile and identify the pivot-zero signed active vector with the exact or computed unnormalized Householder vector under explicit alpha/exact-operation hypotheses. | Build the recursive unnormalized `householderBetaSpec` stored-loop route, prove `normalizedBetaSpecCompactUpdateCompatible` for a stronger rounded model, or replace equality by a perturbation theorem. | checked unnormalized dependency; does not prove normalized self-dot |
| BetaSpec normalization bridge for the unnormalized route | New scalar/vector adapter around the unnormalized route; easy to overclaim as a normalized-loop closure. | `householderBetaSpec_householderVector_eq_householderBetaFromScale_of_ne_zero`, `householderBetaSpec_fl_householderVector_eq_fl_householderBeta_of_exact_add_mul_div_sqrt`, `fl_householderNormalizedVector_eq_householderNormalizedVector_fl_householderVector_betaSpec_of_exact_add_mul_div_sqrt`, and the two `householderTrailingActiveVector_zero_normalized_eq_fl_householderNormalizedVector...` alpha variants compile. | First-pivot signed betaSpec handoff | QR-storage adapter for the corrected unnormalized route; easy to overclaim as full stored-loop closure. | The four `firstStoredPanelStep_fl_householderNormalizedVector_eq_signedActiveBetaSpec...` wrappers compile and combine the betaSpec normalization bridge with the first-pivot stored-panel handoff. | Successor-pivot signed betaSpec handoff | Pivot-1 adapter for the corrected unnormalized route; theorem names could be mistaken for recursive closure. | The four `storedPanelStep_succ_signedActiveBetaSpec_eq_panelFromTopAndTrailing_fl_householderNormalizedVector...exact_add_mul_div_sqrt` wrappers compile and combine the pivot-1 zero-prefix reconstruction with the normalized-to-betaSpec stored-panel handoff. The four matching `...exact_sub_add_mul_div_sqrt` wrappers additionally derive the subtract-zero copy convention from exact subtraction. | Generalize this route through the all-stage stored-loop induction, prove the compatibility surface for a rounded model, or formulate the perturbation version. | checked successor-pivot dependency; exact-sub copy premise removed for exact-operation route; arbitrary rounded route and recursion still open |
| Successor-pivot signed betaSpec tail-leading-block handoff | Premise-reduction adapter for the corrected unnormalized route; theorem names could be mistaken for proving determinant nonbreakdown itself. | The eight `storedPanelStep_succ_signedActiveBetaSpec_eq_panelFromTopAndTrailing_fl_householderNormalizedVector..._of_tail_leadingBlock_det_ne_zero...` wrappers compile and derive the successor nonzero trailing source-column premise from determinant nonbreakdown of `qrLeadingBlock (trailingPanel A)` for computed-alpha/exact-alpha and exact-subtraction surfaces. | Prove the determinant nonbreakdown hypotheses from the stored-loop source conditions at every stage, prove the rounded compatibility surface, or formulate the perturbation version. | checked successor-pivot premise reduction; no arbitrary rounded compatibility or full induction closure |
| Successor betaSpec QR recursion tail-leading-block wrappers | QR-recursion adapter for the corrected unnormalized route; theorem names could be mistaken for proving rounded compatibility. | `successorPanelFirstColumn_ne_zero_of_tail_leadingBlock_det_ne_zero` derives the successor nonzero-column premise from the twice-trailing leading-block determinant, and the computed-alpha/exact-alpha `_of_tail_leadingBlock_det_ne_zero...` QR recursion wrappers compile for both exact-add/mul/div/sqrt and exact-sub/add/mul/div/sqrt surfaces. | Prove the compatibility surface for a rounded model, formulate the perturbation version, or prove the full per-stage source-faithful normalization facts; the tail-leading-block wrappers only remove a redundant nonzero-column caller premise. | checked successor QR dependency; redundant nonzero-column premise removed; arbitrary rounded route still open |
| Compatibility-hypothesis unnormalized handoff | Corrected route surface after the arbitrary-`FPModel` equality was proved false; easy to overclaim as rounded closure if the compatibility predicate is only assumed. | `normalizedBetaSpecCompactUpdateCompatible` names the dot/scale/update operation compatibility needed for the normalized beta-one and unnormalized `householderBetaSpec` compact updates to match. The compact, matrix-rectangular, stored-panel, and first-pivot `..._of_updateCompatible` handoffs compile, `normalizedBetaSpecCompactUpdateCompatible_exactWithUnitRoundoff` proves exact arithmetic satisfies the predicate, `normalizedBetaSpecCompactUpdateCompatible_of_exact_add_mul` proves a smaller exact-add/mul operation surface also suffices, and the direct exact dot/mul plus exact add/mul handoff wrappers expose that sufficient surface at the QR-storage call sites. | Exact-arithmetic unnormalized handoff | Useful for source algebra and exact subcases, but too weak to close a rounded floating-point loop by itself. | `fl_dotProduct_exactWithUnitRoundoff_eq_sum`, `fl_householderScale_exactWithUnitRoundoff_eq`, `fl_householderVector_exactWithUnitRoundoff_eq`, `fl_householderBeta_exactWithUnitRoundoff_eq`, `fl_householderNormalizedVector_self_dot_exactWithUnitRoundoff`, its two-/three-zero variants, the `householderBetaSpec_fl_householderNormalizedVector...eq_one` family, the exact current-layer and recursive-tail full-stage/normalized-loop self-dot-reduction constructors, the exact final-panel self-dot handoffs, `fl_householderApplyCompact_normalized_betaSpec_eq_exactWithUnitRoundoff`, `fl_householderApplyCompactPanel_normalized_betaSpec_eq_exactWithUnitRoundoff`, `fl_householderApplyMatrixRect_normalized_betaSpec_eq_exactWithUnitRoundoff`, `fl_householderStoredPanelStep_normalized_betaSpec_eq_exactWithUnitRoundoff`, and `firstStoredPanelStep_normalized_betaSpec_eq_panelFromTopAndTrailing_exactWithUnitRoundoff` prove the exact model bridge from normalized beta-one updates to unnormalized `householderBetaSpec` matrix-rect/stored-panel updates through the first-pivot QR storage reconstruction and the exact computed/full-stage normalized-vector self-dot/beta-one facts. - **eq (19.13) formed-Q̂ backward error — CLOSED** (`Higham19FormedQ.lean`): `H19_eq19_13_formed_Q_backward_error` (‖Q̂ − Q‖_F ≤ residualAccumBound·√n from `fl_householder_sequence_backward_error` applied to I) + the γ-collapsed `H19_eq19_13_formed_Q_backward_error_gamma` (√n·γ_{r·3(11n+23)}, printed √n·γ̃_{mn}) + opNorm2/Frobenius bridges. This is the FORMED-Q̂ closeness bound (distinct from the MGS stored-loop `mgs_qr_bounds`).
- **MGS stored-loop Theorem 19.13 (`mgs_qr_bounds`) — remains Codex's documented allowed-BLOCKED** (perturbation-bridge route; its own counterexamples rule out naive arbitrary-FPModel equality). **(19.35)-(19.37) QR sensitivity — DEFERRED:** Stewart/Zha perturbation theory absent from Mathlib.
